# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
With recurrence relation questions, the sequence will likely not be arithmetic nor geometric.
Therefore you cannot use series formula ^IISgqEyM

Sequences fit one of three categories (at this level)

Strictly increasing ('increasing')


Strictly decreasing ('decreasing')


Periodic ^pwLYFWvI

A sequence is periodic if the terms repeat in a cycle. The order k of a sequence is how often it repeats. ^PchWwTWc

A sequence is strictly increasing if the terms are always increasing ^JK4ybZSb

A sequence is strictly decreasing if the terms are always decreasing ^L9kTEZW2

periodic ^q2eRidyZ

periodic ^rUgJnZ2F

increasing ^wxXw1Zno

decreasing ^gsOdHlpa

decreasing ^2Xh9clXy

periodic ^xYn6l17k

decreasing ^pofd3VTW

%%
